<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 2.02&#160; Results of Operations
and Financial Condition.</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On September 29, 2004, the Registrant issued a press release and held a
conference call with analysts to report on the results of operations for the
third quarter of fiscal year 2004, which ended on August 31, 2004.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Furnished with this Form
8-K as Exhibit 99.1 is a copy of the press release labeled &#147;McCormick Reports Double-Digit
Earnings Growth on Strong Top Line Results,&#148; which includes an unaudited
Consolidated Income Statement for the three and nine month periods ended August
31, 2004, an unaudited Consolidated Balance Sheet of the Registrant as of
August 31, 2004, and an unaudited consolidated Statement of Cash Flows for the
nine months ended August 31, 2004.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SIGNATURES</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pursuant to the requirements of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934,
the Registrant has duly caused this report to be signed on its behalf by the
undersigned hereunto duly authorized.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">McCORMICK
REPORTS DOUBLE-DIGIT EARNINGS GROWTH ON</font></u></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">STRONG
TOP LINE RESULTS</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SPARKS, MD, SEPTEMBER 29
&#151; McCormick &amp; Company, Incorporated (NYSE:MKC), today reported record third
quarter sales and earnings per share from continuing operations for the quarter
ended August 31, 2004:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Sales increased 10% to $614 million</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Earnings per share from continuing
operations increased 18% to 33</font></b><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#162;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Year-to-date, net cash flow from
continuing operations reached $109 million compared to $19 million a year ago</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales for the quarter
were $614 million, an increase of 10% versus the third quarter of 2003.&#160; Higher volume, pricing and product mix
contributed 7% of the increase, and 3% was added by favorable foreign exchange
rates.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Earnings per share from
continuing operations for the third quarter increased 18% to 33&#162; compared to
28&#162; in the third quarter of 2003.&#160;
Compared to the prior year, gross profit margin was 39.0% versus 38.1%,
and operating income margin was 12.1% versus 11.2%.&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The increase in operating
income margin is net of higher </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">advertising and research and development
expenses.&#160; The Company used a portion of
the proceeds from the settlement of the class action lawsuit received in the
second quarter to fund these marketing and product development efforts.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Year-to-date, net cash
flow from continuing operations was $109 million compared to $19 million in the
prior year.&#160; For the third quarter, net
cash flow from continuing operations rose to $42 million from $6 million a year
ago.&#160; Contributing to the increases for
the quarter and year were higher net income from continuing operations and a
reduction in inventory that is being driven by supply chain initiatives.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Chairman&#146;s Comments</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Robert J. Lawless,
Chairman, President &amp; CEO, commented, &#147;We are extremely pleased with our
third quarter results. These results are a good illustration of our strategy in
action: <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">to improve margins, invest in the
business and grow sales and profits</font></b>.&#160;
With gross profit margin up .9 percentage points, we are creating fuel
for initiatives that include marketing programs, product development and our
B2K program.&#160; These types of investments
are leading to higher sales and profits for both segments of our business.&#160; In the third quarter we increased consumer
sales 12% and industrial sales 9%.&#160;
Profits also increased with operating profit up 18% and net income from
continuing operations up 15%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Our U.S. consumer
business had exceptionally strong sales performance this quarter.&#160; We increased Zatarain&#146;s sales 23% and sales
of other U.S. consumer products 12%.&#160;
This</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>


<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\eudelhofen\04-11026-1\task190711\11026-1-mm.htm',USER='eudelho',CD='Sep 29 07:46 2004' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">performance was driven by
the Zatarain&#146;s rice mixes including the Ready to Serve products introduced
earlier in 2004, and higher sales of grinders, Hispanic products, GrillMates
sauces and blended seasonings.&#160; Pricing
actions, as a result of higher cost vanilla, also contributed to the
increase.&#160; Market conditions in certain
parts of Europe and the Asia/Pacific region are challenging.&#160; In these areas we are focused on maintaining
share and employing multiple strategies for growth.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Sales for the industrial
business continued to strengthen with new products for quick service
restaurants and improved sales of snack seasonings.&#160; In particular, sales of coating systems are
up significantly year-to-date compared to 2003.&#160;
Our ability to develop consumer-preferred flavors is paying off as we
deliver winning products to our customers.&#160;
In international markets, we are shifting our emphasis toward more
value-added, higher-margin products.&#160;
While this initiative is affecting near-term sales performance, in the
long-term it will lead to improved profitability.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Given our year-to-date
results and current financial projections, we expect to increase sales for the
full year at a low double-digit rate.&#160;
Our earnings per share target of $1.51-$1.54 remains unchanged from our
initial goal for 2004.&#160; Net cash flow
from operations after net capital expenditures and dividends will exceed $100
million, and we are using the majority of this cash to repurchase shares during
2004.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;In summary, we have good
momentum as we begin our most significant quarter of the year and are well
positioned with our line-up of products and marketing support for the upcoming
holiday season.&#160; Employees throughout the
Company are working hard to deliver another record year for McCormick in 2004.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Business Segment Results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the third
quarter, sales for McCormick&#146;s consumer business rose 12% when compared to
2003.&#160; Higher volume added 6% to sales,
price and favorable product mix added 3% and favorable foreign exchange added
3%.&#160; In the Americas, sales increased 13%
with volume up 8% and price and product mix adding 5%.&#160; New product success and effective marketing
drove higher volumes during the quarter as well as new distribution gained in
2003 with a major grocery retailer.&#160; In
addition to these volume increases, pricing was higher in the Americas for
vanilla products in response to higher vanilla bean costs<i><font style="font-style:italic;">.&#160; </font></i>Consumer
sales in Europe increased 9% for the quarter, with 8% due to favorable foreign
exchange.&#160; Sales in this region were
affected by more intense competitive conditions.&#160; In the Asia/Pacific region, consumer sales
increased 2%.&#160; Foreign exchange added 5%,
while a less favorable product mix in Australia and an emphasis on
higher-margin products in China led to a net 3% decline in volume, price and
product mix.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Operating income from
continuing operations for the consumer business increased 25% to $57 million
for the third quarter of 2004, despite a $3 million increase in
advertising.&#160; This higher income was
driven by strong sales performance, an emphasis on higher-margin products</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">and cost reduction
efforts.&#160; Operating income margin for the
third quarter rose to 18.7% from 16.7% in the prior year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the third quarter of
2004, sales for McCormick&#146;s industrial business increased 9% when compared to
2003. Higher volume added 5%, favorable foreign exchange added 2% and price and
favorable product mix added 2%.&#160; In the
Americas, industrial sales rose 9% due to an 8% volume increase that was driven
largely by new products.&#160; Industrial
sales in Europe increased 10% for the quarter, with foreign exchange
contributing 11%. A continued shift in emphasis to higher margin products
resulted in reduced sales of certain lower margin products. In the Asia/Pacific
region, industrial sales rose 2% in the third quarter, due to favorable foreign
exchange.&#160; The elimination of certain
bulk ingredient sales offset an increase in sales of more value-added products
during the quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the third quarter of
2004, industrial business operating income increased 12% to $31 million,
despite higher product research and development costs.&#160; This income was the result of higher sales,
an emphasis on more value-added, higher-margin products and cost reduction
efforts.&#160; Operating income margin for the
third quarter rose to 10.1% from 9.7% in the prior year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About McCormick</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">McCormick &amp; Company,
Incorporated is the global leader in the manufacture, marketing and
distribution of spices, seasonings and flavors to the entire food industry &#150; to
foodservice and food processing businesses as well as to retail outlets.</font></p>
